commit 5e2da7ffb39867f4532ab7b209c36d90b2e16913
Author: Chris Novak <chrisnovak@google.com>
Date:   Tue Mar 31 15:59:16 2020 -0700

    Fixes #392 (#394) Visibility attribute for API product not enforced correctly
    
    The Apigee M10n module’s hook_ENTITY_TYPE_access uses the Apigee Monetization API to determine an API Product ‘assign’ access by calling `/developers/{developer}/eligible-products`, which returns AccessResult::allowed for all API products.
    
    This API returns all API Products
    1. That are able to be assigned to an App because the developer purchased a Rate plan that contains the API product
    2. All API products that are not monetized.
    
    Due to #2, the Apigee Edge module hook_ENTITY_TYPE_access needs to return AccessResult::forbidden when the operation is ‘assign’ and the user does not have the correct role to assign an API product to an app.

    controller (proxy) from the storage to make API calls because it can
    only make CRUDL calls.

commit 0f05f8d9f086a3275a8472f6dfa63124e90bc2cd
Author: Dezső Biczó <mxr576@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Jan 8 16:42:26 2018 +0100

    Changes:
    - Added default permissions to developer apps by leveraging
    UncachebleEntityAcccessControllHandler and
    UncacheableEntityPermissionProvider. Entity module added as
    dependency to our module until 8.5.x.
    https://www.drupal.org/project/drupal/issues/2809177
    - As a dependency of the above mentioned handler and provider,
    EntityOwnerInterface had to be implemented on Developer and Developer
    app entities.
    . Apigee Edge developer id is now stored on user entity in a base field.
    - Apigee Edge Developer information is being saved in hook_user_presave
    () instead of hook_user_insert() and hook_user_update().
    Better error logging added to Edge related operations.
